Analysis</title><meta name="description" content="&lt;p&gt;This is a &lt;strong&gt;hands-on, project-based course&lt;/strong&gt; designed to help you learn and apply &lt;strong&gt;essential statistics concepts&lt;/strong&gt; for data analysis and business intelligence. &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Our goal is to &lt;em&gt;simplify&lt;/em&gt; and &lt;em&gt;demystify&lt;/em&gt; the world of statistics using familiar spreadsheet tools like Microsoft Excel, and empower everyday people to understand and apply these tools and techniques – &lt;strong&gt;even if you have absolutely no background in math or stats&lt;/strong&gt;!&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;We&#x27;ll start by discussing the role of statistics in business intelligence, the difference between sample and population data, and the importance of using statistical techniques to make smart predictions and data-driven decisions.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Next we&#x27;ll explore our data using &lt;strong&gt;descriptive statistics&lt;/strong&gt; and &lt;strong&gt;probability distributions&lt;/strong&gt;, introduce the normal distribution and empirical rule, and learn how to apply the &lt;strong&gt;central limit theorem&lt;/strong&gt; to make inferences about populations of any type.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;From there we&#x27;ll practice making estimates with &lt;strong&gt;confidence intervals&lt;/strong&gt;, and using &lt;strong&gt;hypothesis tests&lt;/strong&gt; to evaluate assumptions about unknown population parameters. We&#x27;ll introduce the basic hypothesis testing framework, then dive into concepts like null and alternative hypotheses, t-scores, p-values, type I vs. type II errors, and more.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Last but not least, we&#x27;ll introduce the fundamentals of &lt;strong&gt;regression analysis&lt;/strong&gt;, explore the difference between correlation and causation, and practice using basic linear regression models to make predictions using Excel&#x27;s Analysis Toolpak.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Throughout the course, you&#x27;ll play the role of a Recruitment Analyst for &lt;strong&gt;Maven Business School&lt;/strong&gt;. Your goal is to use the statistical techniques you&#x27;ve learned to explore student data, predict the performance of future classes, and propose changes to help improve graduate outcomes.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;You&#x27;ll also practice applying your skills to &lt;strong&gt;5 real-world BONUS PROJECTS&lt;/strong&gt;, and use statistics to explore data from restaurants, medical centers, pharmaceutical companys, safety teams, airlines, and more.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;COURSE OUTLINE:&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ul&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Why Statistics?&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ul&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;Discuss the role of statistics in the context of business intelligence and decision-making, and introduce the statistics workflow&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Understanding Data with Descriptive Statistics&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ul&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;Understand data using descriptive statistics in Excel, including frequency distributions and measures of central tendency &amp;amp; variability&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;PROJECT #1&lt;/strong&gt;: Maven Pizza Parlor&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Modeling Data with Probability Distributions&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ul&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;Model data with probability distributions, and use the normal distribution to calculate probabilities and make value estimates using Excel formulas&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;PROJECT #2&lt;/strong&gt;: Maven Medical Center&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;The Central Limit Theorem&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ul&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;Introduce the Central Limit Theorem, which leverages the normal distribution to make inferences on populations with any distribution&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Making Estimates with Confidence Intervals&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ul&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;Make estimates with confidence intervals, which use sample statistics to define a range where an unknown population parameter likely lies&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;PROJECT #3&lt;/strong&gt;: Maven Pharma&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Drawing Conclusions with Hypothesis Tests&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ul&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;Draw conclusions with hypothesis tests, which let you evaluate assumptions about population parameters using sample statistics&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;PROJECT #4&lt;/strong&gt;: Maven Safety Council&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Making Predictions with Regression Analysis&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ul&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;Make predictions with regression analysis, and estimate the values of a dependent variable via its relationship with independent to evaluate assumptions about unknown population parameters. We&#x27;ll introduce the basic hypothesis testing framework, then dive into concepts like null and alternative hypotheses, t-scores, p-values, type I vs. type II errors, and more.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Last but not least, we&#x27;ll introduce the fundamentals of &lt;strong&gt;regression analysis&lt;/strong&gt;, explore the difference between correlation and causation, and practice using basic linear regression models to make predictions using Excel&#x27;s Analysis Toolpak.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Throughout the course, you&#x27;ll play the role of a Recruitment Analyst for &lt;strong&gt;Maven Business School&lt;/strong&gt;. data-purpose="requirements-title" class="title ud-heading-xl">Requirements</h2><ul class="ud-unstyled-list ud-block-list"><li><div class="ud-block-list-item ud-block-list-item-small ud-block-list-item-tight ud-block-list-item-neutral ud-text-sm"><svg aria-label="" role="img" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-xsmall ud-icon-color-neutral ud-block-list-item-icon"><use xlink:href="#icon-bullet"></use></svg><div class="ud-block-list-item-content">No math or stats background is required – we&#x27;ll start with the absolute basics!</div></div></li><li><div class="ud-block-list-item ud-block-list-item-small ud-block-list-item-tight ud-block-list-item-neutral ud-text-sm"><svg aria-label="" role="img" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-xsmall demos</div></div></li></ul></div><div class="ud-text-sm component-margin" data-purpose="course-description"><h2 data-purpose="description-title" class="ud-heading-xl course-description-module-scss-module___l52bq__description-header">Description</h2><div class="_container_kolij_42" data-expanded="false"><div class="_content_kolij_32 _with-gradient_kolij_57" style="max-height:13.8125rem"><div tabindex="-1"><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:description:description" data-testid="safely-set-inner-html:description:description"><p>This is a <strong>hands-on, project-based course</strong> designed to help you learn and apply <strong>essential statistics concepts</strong> for data analysis and business intelligence. </p><p><br /></p><p>Our goal is to <em>simplify</em> and <em>demystify</em> the world of statistics using familiar spreadsheet tools like Microsoft Excel, and empower everyday people to understand and apply these tools and techniques – <strong>even if you have absolutely no background in math or stats</strong>!</p><p><br /></p><p>We'll start by discussing the role of statistics in business intelligence, the difference between sample and population data, and the importance of using statistical techniques to make smart predictions and data-driven decisions.</p><p><br /></p><p>Next we'll explore our data using <strong>descriptive statistics</strong> and <strong>probability distributions</strong>, introduce the normal distribution and empirical rule, and learn how to apply the <strong>central limit theorem</strong> to make inferences about populations of any type.</p><p><br /></p><p>From there we'll practice making estimates with <strong>confidence intervals</strong>, and using <strong>hypothesis tests</strong> to evaluate assumptions about unknown population parameters. We'll introduce the basic hypothesis testing framework, then dive into concepts like null and alternative hypotheses, t-scores, p-values, type I vs. type II errors, and more.</p><p><br /></p><p>Last but not least, we'll introduce the fundamentals of <strong>regression analysis</strong>, explore the difference between correlation and causation, and practice using basic linear regression models to make predictions using Excel's Analysis Toolpak.</p><p><br /></p><p>Throughout the course, you'll play the role of a Recruitment Analyst for <strong>Maven Business School</strong>. Your goal is to use the statistical techniques you've learned to explore student data, predict the performance of future classes, and propose changes to help improve graduate outcomes.</p><p><br /></p><p>You'll also practice applying your skills to <strong>5 real-world BONUS PROJECTS</strong>, and use statistics to explore data from restaurants, medical centers, pharmaceutical companys, safety teams, airlines, and more.</p><p><br /></p><p><strong>COURSE OUTLINE:</strong></p><p><br /></p><ul><li><p><strong>Why Statistics?</strong></p><ul><li><p><em>Discuss the role of statistics in the context of business intelligence and decision-making, and introduce the statistics workflow</em></p></li></ul><p><br /></p></li><li><p><strong>Understanding Data with Descriptive Statistics</strong></p><ul><li><p><em>Understand data using descriptive statistics in Excel, including frequency distributions and measures of central tendency &amp; variability</em></p></li><li><p><strong>PROJECT #1</strong>: Maven Pizza Parlor</p></li></ul><p><br /></p></li><li><p><strong>Modeling Data with Probability Distributions</strong></p><ul><li><p><em>Model data with probability distributions, and use the normal distribution to calculate probabilities and make value estimates using Excel formulas</em></p></li><li><p><strong>PROJECT #2</strong>: Maven Medical Center</p></li></ul><p><br /></p></li><li><p><strong>The Central Limit Theorem</strong></p><ul><li><p><em>Introduce the Central Limit Theorem, which leverages the normal distribution to make inferences on populations with any distribution</em></p></li></ul><p><br /></p></li><li><p><strong>Making Estimates with Confidence Intervals</strong></p><ul><li><p><em>Make estimates with confidence intervals, which use sample statistics to define a range where an unknown population parameter likely lies</em></p></li><li><p><strong>PROJECT #3</strong>: Maven Pharma</p></li></ul><p><br /></p></li><li><p><strong>Drawing Conclusions with Hypothesis Tests</strong></p><ul><li><p><em>Draw conclusions with hypothesis tests, which let you evaluate assumptions about population parameters using sample statistics</em></p></li><li><p><strong>PROJECT #4</strong>: Maven Safety Council</p></li></ul><p><br /></p></li><li><p><strong>Making Predictions with Regression Analysis</strong></p><ul><li><p><em>Make predictions with regression analysis, and estimate the values of a dependent variable via its relationship with independent variables</em></p></li><li><p><strong>PROJECT #5</strong>: Maven Airlines</p></li></ul></li></ul><p><br /></p><p>Join today and get <strong>immediate, lifetime access </strong>to the following:</p><p><br /></p><ul><li><p><em>7.5 hours of high-quality video</em></p></li><li><p><em>Statistics for Data Analysis PDF ebook (150+ pages)</em></p></li><li><p><em>Downloadable Excel project files &amp; solutions</em></p></li><li><p><em>Expert support and Q&amp;A forum</em></p></li><li><p><em>30-day Udemy satisfaction guarantee</em></p></li></ul><p><br /></p><p>If you're a data analyst, data scientist, business intelligence professional, or anyone looking to use statistics to make smart, data-driven decisions, <strong>this course is for you</strong>!</p><p><br /></p><p>Happy learning!</p><p>-Enrique Ruiz <em>(Lead Statistics &amp; Excel Instructor, </em><strong><em>Maven Analytics</em></strong><em>)</em></p><p><br /></p><p>__________</p><p><strong>Looking for our full course library?</strong> Search "<strong>Maven Analytics</strong>" to browse our full collection of
